 In such a situation, tax will be deducted at the rate of 2 percent
 ek karod rupye par bank 2 lakh rupye tex kaatega or sarkaar ko jamaa kara degaa
 He further explained that the government has introduced section 194N in the Finance Bill (finance Bill) that if a person or institution withdraws one crore or more from the bank account from the bank, then the government has allowed banks to deduct TDS at 2 per cent
 However, this tax is not only for lump sum withdrawal but also on total withdrawal
 " Kolkata Knight Riders defeated Royal Challengers Bangalore by five wickets on Sunday in the 60th match of the sixth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL)
 ranchi main jharkhand cricket sangh stadium kii dhimi pich par royal chalangers kii raftaar rokane main kolkata nite rides kaamyaab rahe
 The four leading bowlers of the Knight Riders bowled tightly, batting the bat of explosive batsmen like Bangalore's Chris Gayle, Virat Kohli and Abraham de Villiers
 bengalooru nirdhaarit 20 overon main nau wicket par 115 ran hi bana sakaa jise nite rides ne paanch wicket shesh rahete hasil kar liya
 Jacques Kallis was adjudged Player of the Match
 kalis ne gendbaaji karte hue jahaan 17 ran dekar do wicket hasil kiye vahiin lakshya kaa peechha karte hue nite rides ko sarvaadhik 41 ranon kaa yogadan bhi diya
 The Knight Riders also had a slow start and on the second ball of the first over, Manvinder Bisla was caught by Moises Henriques without opening the account
 iske baad sanbhalkar khelte hue captain gautam gambhir (14) ne jacks kalis ke saath 31 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Gambhir caught Chris Gayle off the fifth ball of the sixth over
 iske baad tisare wicket ke liye kalis or yusuf pathan (18) ne 30 ranon kii saajhedaari kii
 Pathan was trapped lbw by Murali Karthik off the third ball of the 11th over
 kalis ne sanyam se khelte hue chauthe wicket ke liye manoj tiwari (24) ke saath chauthe wicket kii saajhedaari main 35 ran jode
 Kallis faced 45 balls with four boundaries
 kalis ko abhimanyu mithun ne 17wein over kii chauthi gend par henrics ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 When Kallis was out, the Knight Riders had a score of 96 runs and they needed the same number of runs in 20 balls to win, which the Knight Riders got by five wickets with four balls remaining
 bengalooru ke liye ravi rampaul tathaa karthik ne kasi hui gendbaaji kii or ek-ek wicket bhi chatkaaye
 But the remaining Bangalore bowlers could not save such an easy target
 vinay kumaar ko do wicket mila
 Earlier, the Bangalore batsmen played very slow and scored 115 runs for nine wickets in the scheduled 20 overs
 royal chalangers ne shuruaati 10 overon main salaami ballebaaj cheteshwar pujaara (5) or captain viraat kohli (17) ke wicket ganvaa die
 Pujara got Suchitra Senanayake caught by Laxmipathy Balaji for a total of 15 runs
 kohli ne gail ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 25 gendon par 31 ran jode
 Kohli looked in rhythm, but was bowled by Jacques Kallis on a total of 46
 kohli 14 gendon par do chauke lagaae
 Gayle looked to be at the crease after scoring 33 runs and was expected to show a quick hand to Bengaluru, but he was stumped on the first ball of the 14th over brought by Sunil Nairin
 apni visphotak style ke vipareet gail ne 36 gendon kaa saamana kar ek chaukaa or ek chakka lagaaya
 After the Gayle, Abraham de Villiers (28) was just getting in the form of Rau that Laxmipathy kept walking behind the wicket in a round of reverse sweep from Balaji
 isse thik pehle vaali gend par divilliars ne chakka lagaaya tha
 After de Villiers left Bangalore were able to score 20 runs after losing five wickets in the final 25 balls
 nite rides ke liye nairine ne chaar tathaa balaji or jacks kalis ne do-do wicket hasil kiye
 With this win, Bengaluru's hopes of reaching the second position remained undefeated and with 16 points from 14 matches, they are still fourth in the points table
 tippaniyan For Kolkata, on the other hand, this victory may not be special in terms of scoring and remaining in the tournament, but he managed to avenge the previous defeat at the hands of Bengaluru
 kolkata ke 14 maichon main 12 ank ho gaye tathaa ankatalika main uski sthiti chathe paaydaan par he
 Kolkata Knight Riders managed to stop the pace of Royal Challengers on the slow pitch of Jharkhand Cricket Association Stadium in Ranchi
 nite rides ke chaaron pramukh gendbaajon ne kasi hui gendbaaji karte hue bengalooru ke kris gail, viraat kohli or abraham divilliars jaise visphotak ballebaajon ke balle ko shant kar diya
 Bengaluru could only manage 115 runs for nine wickets in the stipulated 20 overs, which was achieved by the Knight Riders with five wickets remaining
 jacks kalis ko plir of da match chunaa gaya
 While Kallis took two wickets for 17 runs while bowling, chasing the target also contributed 41 runs to the Knight Riders
 nite rides kii shuruyaat bhi dhimi rahi tathaa pehle hi over kii duusari gend par manvinder bislaa bina khaataa khole moysis henrics ko kaich thama baithe
 After this, captain Gautam Gambhir (14) played a fine 31-run partnership with Jacques Kallis
 chathe over kii paanchavin gend par gambhir ne kris gail ko kaich thama diya
 After this, Kallis and Yusuf Pathan (18) shared a 30-run partnership for the third wicket
 pathan ko 11wein over kii teesri gend par murali karthik ne pagabaadha out diya
 Kallis, playing sparingly, added 35 runs for the fourth wicket partnership with Manoj Tiwari (24)
 kalis ne 45 gendon kaa saamana kar chaar chauke lagaae
 Kallis was caught by Abhimanyu Mithun on the fourth ball of the 17th over at the hands of Henriques
 kalis jab out hue to nite rides kaa score 96 ran tha or unhen jeet ke liye 20 gendon main itane hi ranon kii jarurat thi, jise nite rides ne chaar gend shesh rahete paanch wicket se hasil kar liya
 Ravi Rampaul and Karthik bowled tightly for Bangalore and took one wicket each
 lekin itane aasaan lakshya ko bangalore ke shesh gendbaaj bachaa nahin sake
 Vinay Kumar got two wickets
 isse pehle, bengalooru ke ballebaajon ne kaaphi dhimaa khelaa or nirdhaarit 20 overon main nau wicket par 115 ran banaae
 Royal Challengers lost opener Cheteshwar Pujara (5) and captain Virat Kohli (17) in the opening 10 overs
 pujaara ko 15 ran ke kul yoga par suchithra senanayake ne lakshmipathi balaji ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 Kohli added 31 runs off 25 balls for the second wicket with Gayle
 kohli lay main najar aa rahe the, lekin 46 ke kul yoga par jacks kalis ne unhen bold kar diya
 Kohli hit two fours off 14 balls
 gail 33 ran banaakar krij par tikte lag rahe the or unase bengalooru ko abhi tej haath dikhaane kii ummid thi, lekin sunil nairine dwaara laae gaye 14wein over kii pehali gend par vah stump out ho gaye
 Unlike his explosive style, Gayle faced 36 balls with a four and a six
 gail ke baad abraham divilliars (28) abhi rau main aate lag hi rahe the ki lakshmipathi balaji kii gend par reverse sweep karne ke chakkar main wicket ke peeche kaich thama kar chalate bane
 De Villiers hit a six just before that
 divilliars ke jane ke baad bangalore antim 25 gendon main paanch wicket ganvaakar 20 ran hi bana sakaa
 For the Knight Riders, Nairin took four wickets and Balaji and Jacques Kallis took two wickets each
 is jeet ke saath hi bengalooru kii duusare paaydaan par pahunchane kii ummid bachi rah gai tathaa 14 maichon main 16 ank ke saath abhi bhi vah ankatalika main chauthe paaydaan par hi he
 The comments duusari taraf kolkata ke liye yah jeet ankatalika or toornament main bane rahane ke lihaaj se bhale kuch khaas na ho lekin bengalooru ke haathon mili pichhali haar kaa badla lene main vah kaamyaab rahaa
 Kolkata has 12 points from 14 matches and their position is sixth in the table
 bengalooru nirdhaarit 20 overon main nau wicket par 115 ran hi bana sakaa jise nite rides ne paanch wicket shesh rahete hasil kar liya

 Mouth blisters are very painful
 munh ke andruni hisse main hone vaale se chhaale kai kaarnon se ho jate hai
 Many times they emerge due to a lack of clean stomach, due to worsening of hormonal balance, injury, periods or due to cosmetic surgery
 haalanki bazaar main ise thik karne keliye kai tarah kii davaaiyaan maujuud hai lekin kai baar in dawaaiyon kaa galessar bhi ho jaataa he
 In such a situation, it is better that you adopt home remedies
 1
 Garlic is very effective for treating blisters using garlic
 do se teen lahasun kii kaliyaan lekar unka ek paste bana len
 Now apply this paste on the affected area
 lagane ke 15 minute baad use dho len
 The anti-biotic properties present in garlic helps the ulcers heal quickly
 2
 Tea tree oil tree oil has anti-bacterial properties
 chhaalon ke upar inhen lagane se bahut jaldi phayda hota he
 Applying it three to four times a day to the affected area will help
 3
 The use of ice can be beneficial very quickly by applying cold cheese on the skins
 saath hi ye dard or sujan ko bhi kam karne kaa kam karata he
 4
 doodh kaa prayogdoodh main calcium maujuud hota he jo virus se ladane kaa kaam karata he
 Also actively participates in the healing process
 thande doodh main rooyee bhigonkar prabhavit jagah par lagane se phayda hoga
 5
 alovera bhi degaa rahatelovera ke istemaal se prabhavit jagah kii jalan kam ho jaati he
 Also, the chemical substances present in aloe vera help to heal the wound quickly

 ) Lord Parshuram was born on Akshaya Tritiya, hence Parshuram Jayanti is celebrated on Akshaya Tritiya
 parashuram ji kii gananaa dashavataron main hoti he
 Parshuram is giving special information on the birth anniversary of Shri Kashi Vishwanath Temple, Varanasi Trust Member, Pandit Prasad Dixit - Lord Parshuram himself is part of Lord Vishnu
 baishakh maas ke shukla paksh kii tritiya tithi ko punarvasu nakshatra main raatri ke pratham prahar main ucch ke grahon se yukt mithun raashi par rahu ke sthit rahete mata renuka ke garbh se bhagwaan parashuram kaa pradurbhaav hua tha
 Akshaya Tritiya is believed to be the birth of Lord Parashurama
 is tithi ko pradosh vyapini rup main grahan karnaa chahie kyonki bhagwaan parashuram kaa prakatya kaal pradosh kaal hi he
 This time Parshuram Jayanti is being celebrated on 18 April 2018
 akshay tritiya par raashi anusaar karen ye kharidari, hoga laabh hi lapaise naam padaa tha parashurambhagwan parashuram maharishi jamadagni ke putr the
 His mother and Vishwamitra's mother had received prasad for the sake of sonship, which was transformed into one by the Dev Shastra
 isse renuka kaa putr parashuram ji brahman hote hue bhi kshatriya swabhaav ke the jabaki vishwamitra ji kshatriya kul main utpann hokar bhi brahmarshi ho gaye 
 At the time when he was incarnated, Kshatriya kings had become dominant on the earth
 unhi main se ek raja ne unke pita jamadagni kaa vadh kar diya tha, jisase cruddh hokar inhone 21 baar dushton raajaaon se prithvi ko mukt kiya
 He got the name Parashurama due to wearing the parshu given to him by Lord Shiva
 pita kii ajna kaa maan rakhane ke liye parashuram ko apni hi mata kaa vadh karnaa padaa tha
 He revived his mother by seeking a boon from his father
 aaj ke din vrati nity- karm se nivrutt ho praatah snaan karke suryaast tak maun rahe or snaan karke bhagwaan parashuram kii murti kaa shodashopchaar pujan karen tathaa raatri jaagran kar is vrath main shri ram-mantra kaa jap karnaa sarvshereshth hota he
